A must try!!!
This place is a hidden gem. The crazy blend of flavours with the intricate simplicity of cooking was outstanding. However, the food isn't the only thing out of the world at this place, the serene ambiance and the calm and caring hospitality in the lap of the mountains makes it a hell of an experience.
Couldn't go wrong at this placeüòá.

PS - Don't go here when you are in a hurry, the service is slow because of the freshness of the food and the wait is totally worth it.< /review>

< Review>
Phenomenal food! If you‚Äôre passing by and have some time to spare, there aren‚Äôt any better restaurants within fifty miles.
They hand make every order from scratch and have only one chef, so it‚Äôs definitely a bit of a wait. To make up for it they have a beautiful patio to wait at, you can call in your order, or you can even wait in your car.
My wife and I elected to wait in the car, and because we said we were hungry when ordering they brought each individual dish out to us the moment it was ready, instead of waiting for everything to be done. Truly superb food, service, and attitudes. We‚Äôre definitely going back!< /Review>

<user_id>116891586429392790410< /user_id><time>1605505148756<//time><response>None< /response><Text>Yes, the food is delicious. Do YOU have 2.5 hours for dinner? We do not have any choices for vegan food on the mountain, let alone good vegan good. This place has it. More than you can ever imagine.
If ANY restaurant has served everyone in a party, appetizers, entree‚Äôs, desert, and the final bill comes and one person ( me) whom was there for their birthday and who ordered first was not served their dinner because they forgot, THAT makes for a very unpleasant experience. Being gracious I said YES I would still like my dinner. The seating was outside and, by this time, everyone were freezing(temp. In the 30‚Äôs) but all set outside waiting for me to finally have my dinner over an hour after everyone else had finished.
BUT, I was charged for my dinner.
The expectation is, of course, that you pay for the food that you eat. That would be assuming everyone is served during the same time frame as liberal as that should be. If all people in a party ( 5 in this instance) have to wait until all have finished eating ant then wait for one more person in that party to begin their dinner order, that dinner order should be complimentary.
Did I eat the food, yes. Was it good, yes. Was it painful for 4 others to sit outside in 30 degree weather for an hour to wait for one person to eat, yes.
In my opinion, this place owes me one free dinner. My advice to anyone going here is to request visual confirmation that their order is being cooked. If not, you too may not receive dinner for hours after you have ordered and everyone else in your party has finished like me.

< Text>
Lovely place in Frasier park, great place to stop by on your way to LA (or back). A bit pricey but the food is fully vegetarian, organic, healthy, filling and palatable. The owners/servers are really kind and explain the significance of the restaurant with all the different options and give their recommendations. There's space for around 40 people (officially, although the place looks like it can seat half of that) and there's a child's playhouse too. You can buy some of their home made ghee and other things for sale. Overall, excellent food and service!<//Text>

< review>
Great hospitality.Really appreciate the warm welcome and great views.The snow clad mountains were a spectacular view .They even gave bananas at the end of the meal to carry along for the way which was a sweet gesture.

However food was not upto the mark.The aaloo parantha lacked flavor.We had ordered the cheese jalapeno paratha but due to a mix up in the kitchen they offered us aaloo parantha.The mint chutney though tasted fresh did not taste like a traditional mint chutney. The Malaysian thupka was very spicy.The service was delayed and took nearly 35 minutes to get the food although we were the only customers at that point.

If you wish to experience great views and heartwarming hospitality visit this place, however the food was below expectation in our case.They do offer great variety in menu though</review>

<review>The Red Dot is hard to explain.¬† I love places like this because you can not describe it, but 100% (maybe 200%) worth the effort to get here.¬† We started with a hand made pizza.¬† Actually we biked to the restaurant from I-5 all the way up a long hill in a single gear bike. ¬† We called ahead to check hours and after making sure they were open the cafe suggested that we order our appetizer now and it will be ready when we got there. ¬† Thank God for that, it was a long hill and by the time we got there we devoured the pizza. ¬†We sat outside in our bike gear and ordered a few more things Tofu Curry, finally Pad Thai.¬† All made to order all excellent!

I was reading a few things about the cafe and Frazier Park California.¬† Everything was calm, polite, easy going everywhere we went.¬† At first I thought I was transported back to the 60's into a hippie commune.¬† Then I though a cult had taken over the town. ¬† On both cases I was wrong.¬† Just friendly people far enough away from LA, SF and other cities to remind you that Life Is Good.

So please take the time and go out of your way to eat and visit a wonderful place with wonderful people and wonderful food.

Oh yeah, I kept forgetting to take pictures of the food. ¬†When ever the food showed up we dug right in. ¬†By the time I remembered to take a picture either there was nothing ¬†left...nothing, or the picture‚Äã would not have photographed well. ¬† Yes no pictures = we licked the bowl...Really!

We did not get dessert, we usually do not but was tempted. ¬†We were surprised to get 2 delicious bananas, truly unexpected and awesome.

< Text>
Exaggerated reviews? Not for this place. Because the food is made by hand for each other, it is amazing. And yes, it did have a bit of a wait, but it's not from pre-cut, pre-portioned veggies in a baggie; this is the real deal. 100% vegetarian and as an omnivore, had that not been part of the title of the restaurant and some of the dishes, I would not have known that my "beef" shwarma was a beef substitute; it honestly had a better texture and I caught myself wondering when I was going to bite into a piece of gristle and was surprised when I didn't. That's how true to taste this place is. 11/5 stars.</Text>

What kind of office takes money before the procedure when they are supposedly certain the patient would need the procedure. I was only comfortable paying half of it. So I paid half and my insurance and got the deep clean done. It was excruciatingly painful way more painful then I remember getting it done a decade ago. Anyways, my insurance covered it, because I've had a deep clean a decade ago.

This is why they collect money up front so you lock into doing the procedure. They rush you into doing the deep clean within the week so they don't have to file the preauthorization with the insurance company, because I called my insurance the day after the office said I needed a deep clean, all the office has to do is file a predetermination claim with the insurance. This box is pretty great. They go through the movements and have plenty of modifications to make sure you don't get hurt or frustrated about the movements in the workout. They are more of a traditional box, but not in the sense that they require you to vomit and go into rhabdo to be a part of the box.

< Text>
Fantastic vegan Vietnamese food at a place that is a bit run down, but you won‚Äôt be disappointed by the flavors and textures. I had the fried rice with 2 main dish choices for $9 and an even $10 with a Soda. Cash only.

Staff are friendly and its fun to listen to them speaking Vietnamese amongst themselves and with some local regulars.

The owner said he opened this shop more than 35 years ago after coming from Vietnam. The vegan ‚Äòmeats‚Äô were originally made using bananas, but they now use soy base or jackfruit.

The vegan kebabs and chicken were really tasty and filling. I‚Äôd been frustrated by the lack of vegetarian options when I visited Vietnam in the 90‚Äôs, but the owners assured me I would find a lot of great options now. Such friendly people.

For sustainability, eat-in diners on reusable plates and utensils but to-go in plastic packaging in plastic bags it seems (so bring your own to save in take-out waste if you can).<//Text>

<review>First off, it's great to know that this small whole in the wall is trying to do veggie/vegan vietnamese.

It came recommend from a friend and unfortunately it did not meet the hype and expectations.

I was disappointed to experience difficulty navigating and understanding their menu. While the food is "cheap" it lacked in flavor and freshness.

I visited around the lunch hour and it was evident that the food had been sitting around from the AM. I chose to try their Sesame Veggie Chicken Sandwich. I was pleasantly surprised when a fresh roll of bread was placed in the oven to crisp up. That's where the glam of the sandwich ended. Next the "meat" was pre-made and microwaved to serve. The "meat" lacked flavor and quickly became cold.

Additionally, I ordered their Summer Rolls. I was happy that a range of "meats" where inside the rolls. The sauce that accompanied the rolls was the one thing that saved both my rolls and sandwich.

I do not plan to return. I think the idea is great and as a vegetarian, I am always looking for new and creative ways to enjoy food. Tofoo; however, did not live up to its hype and at best, I didn't even "get what I paid for."<//review><pictures>None</pictures><resp>None</resp>< gmapID>

<GmapID>0x80c2be2d45ef6561:0x3791939344a1375d</GmapID><Pictures>None</Pictures><time>1596952241626<//time><Rate>5<//Rate><UserId.>114468858816761172438<//UserId.></record></dataset><record>
<Text>Great New find; you can see and taste the quality. A simple menu with complex flavors & food that will keep you coming back! Although our server was great everyone came and checked on us. The bartender was mixing Valentine's Day concoctions and recruited us to participate in a taste test.

The medium-sized room is elegantly decorated. The bathrooms are large and clean. We arrived for an early dinner, the place was mostly empty. By 6:30 every table was full & there were hungry patrons waiting for a seat. Others picked up to-go orders, so people already know about Lotus and Light. I recommend you check it out, and review it for yourself.

Parking is ample & next door to Starbucks. You can enjoy some shopping or hit the grocery market a few doors down. I highly recommend the 50/50 beef and pork rice (it's not on the menu as 50/50). The meat was so tender and flavorful the sauce included was on point.

I had the beef pho my wife had the vegetable tofu. Mine was rich and flavorful I thought hers was a little bland. Overall everything we sampled was fantastic. The service was great. As you can see on receipt, the price is what you would expect. The quality excellent, the space was bright and clean. I give 5 stars with confidence I will be back save me a table!< /Text><Rating>5< /Rating>< resp>

<userid>102050855867682345400< /userid><user_name>Kendra Vander Vliet</user_name>< Time>
1528848398187<//Time>
<Rating>5< /Rating><Review>If you love Golden Deli in San Gabriel you'll love this place more. It's great that I finally don't have to drive all the way to the SGV to get my fix of authentic pho.

What makes this particular pho place stand out from the billion of other pho places in Los Angeles is how darn clean their pho tastes. It doesn't have any MSG, they either use no salt or very little so you can apply your own level of sodium chloride to your liking. The best part of it is the pho broth is SO DANG rich and perfect it doesn't need anything extra. This place has unexpectedly become my new favorite restaurant after a workout. It always makes my body feel like I'm filling it with nutrients and not just a pho equivalent of nightQuil that I need to lay down to digest for several hours after eating.

The same level of rich brothness is the same for their for their veggie pho. The broth is an incredibly rich umami shiitake broth. I've never had a veggie pho that the broth ever stood out like that. It's really really good. They also must steam their veggies over broth because all the steamed veggies were full of the same rich broth flavor. It's as good as their beef pho.

This is also the only pho place that I'll eat tendon in my pho. I appreciate that they cut it up into edible small bite size pieces that are appealing and easy to eat.

Their crunchy wraps and veggie spring roll wraps are also killer. The prices are also very fair for the level of quality you get.

Another small thing that is nice. The noodles in the pho are cooked to order. Have you ever been to a restaurant when you get your pho you have to try to separate all the noodles from being stuck together in a dense ball because they were prepared an hour ago? You won't have that problem here.</Review>< pictures>
None</pictures>
